GPT-Red：以自我博弈解锁鲁棒性自我提升

GPT-Red: Unlocking Self-Improvement for Robustness

了解 OpenAI 的自动化红队系统 GPT-Red——它通过自我博弈（self-play）提升 AI 安全性、对齐水平及对提示注入（prompt injection）的鲁棒性。

英文原文 EN

Explore GPT-Red, OpenAI’s automated red teaming system that uses self-play to improve AI safety, alignment, and prompt injection robustness.

洞察Safety/robustness 已经从合规成本变成主线模型的性能护城河：谁的红队自动化更强，谁就能更快把新能力放行到生产。OpenAI 把 red-teaming 从『Trust & Safety 组的重复劳动』重构为一条可扩展的模型工程 pipeline，等同于把一批资深 red-teamer / RLHF / adversarial ML 人才的隐性经验产品化。近期从事 jailbreak 研究、adversarial robustness、RL-based safety 训练的人在 OpenAI/Anthropic/DeepMind 之间流动性显著上升。
招聘行动① 立刻追踪 GPT-Red / Preparedness / Trustworthy AI 团队公开署名（近半年论文+博客+GitHub commit）建立候选池；② 在 Anthropic『Alignment Science』、DeepMind『AGI Safety』、Meta『Responsible AI』做对标 mapping，优先锁定既懂 attack 又懂后训练/RLHF 的双料 IC；③ 把『GPT-Red 类自演化红队』写进 JD 关键词，用于精准触达 Scale AI / Apollo Research / METR / Redwood 的核心研究员。
OpenAI Blog · Wed, 15 Ju 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier Radar社区/其他开源工具技术社区/论文推理训练方法开源生态产品方向

Thinking Machines Lab/tinker-cookbook - 使用 Tinker 做后训练的官方指南

thinking-machines-lab/tinker-cookbook — Post-training with Tinker

Mira Murati 创立的 Thinking Machines Lab 发布 Tinker 后训练框架的官方 cookbook，覆盖 SFT、偏好对齐、RL、蒸馏等主流后训练范式的最佳实践与端到端脚本，单日 +100 stars，是新兴前沿实验室在开源侧的重要动作。

洞察TML 长期以低调著称，其首次官方 cookbook 更像是招人信号弹——他们在明确对外展示后训练全栈能力，说明团队进入需要以 IC 密度换产品出货速度的阶段。类似曲线在 2024 年 Anthropic、2025 年 xAI 都出现过，通常伴随随后 3-6 个月的密集 hiring 窗口。
招聘行动将 TML 现有署名工程师（GitHub commit + 论文作者顺序 + LinkedIn 头衔一致比对）做 mapping；同时在 OpenAI Post-training、Anthropic RLHF、DeepMind Reward Modeling 三条线做重叠画像。对候选人主打『去中量级前沿实验室做 RL/后训练 IC』的差异化叙事。

未来的实验室应像数据中心——Lila Sciences 的 Andy Beam 与 Rafa Gómez-Bombarelli

The Lab of the Future Should Feel Like a Data Center — Andy Beam & Rafa Gómez-Bombarelli, Lila Sciences

Latent Space 对话 Lila Sciences 的 CTO Andy Beam 与首席科学官 Rafa Gómez-Bombarelli，讨论一个核心押注：'科学，而非互联网，才是最后一片未被开采的训练数据金矿'。Lila 运营着一个 AI 引导、7×24 小时不间断运转的机器人实验室，覆盖生物、化学、药物发现和材料科学，目标是打造直接接入湿实验室的'科学超级智能'。对话涵盖把实验室当作数据中心来设计、把强化学习作为数据生成方法并以自然作为验证器、他们已积累的 10 万亿级'经实验验证的推理 token'库，以及生物 vs 材料科学谁更难等前沿命题。

洞察AI-for-Science 已经进入『系统工程化』阶段，招人重心从 pure ML 转向 wet-lab 自动化+机器人+基础模型的跨界复合。这类岗位薪酬弹性最大，但人才池极窄——熟悉 Ginkgo、Recursion、Isomorphic、Xaira、Nabla 的候选人是关键节点。
招聘行动整理 Lila / Isomorphic Labs / Recursion / Genesis / Xaira 五家 AI-for-Science 头部实验室的核心 IC 表，交叉重叠比对（每家 30-80 人，去重后约 200-300 人）；对国内医药 AI、Ginkgo 类合成生物公司里同类背景候选人做主动触达，抢先做窗口期布局。
Latent Space · 2026-07-16 原文 ↗

认识 GPT-Red：OpenAI 打造的用于加固自家模型的 LLM 超级黑客

Meet GPT-Red: an LLM super-hacker OpenAI built to make its models safer

MIT Technology Review 高级 AI 编辑 Will Douglas Heaven 深度报道 OpenAI 自研的红队模型 GPT-Red——一个通过自博弈自动挖掘攻击方法、专门用来加固其他模型的攻防型 LLM。GPT-Red 发现了名为'伪造思维链'的新型提示注入攻击（在受害模型的推理笔记中植入虚假条目），并在重跑 2025 年基准时超过人类红队；针对 GPT-5 的强攻击超过 90% 有效，但对 GPT-5.6 的成功率降至不到 23%。OpenAI 在模拟真实部署环境的'道场'中训练 GPT-Red，包含浏览器、邮件日历和代码编辑器等工具，官方表态称其只作为人类红队的补充而非替代，且不会对外发布。

洞察这是难得的『组织架构级信号』——它显性揭示了 OpenAI 已经把 safety 从横向部门重组成纵向嵌入主线训练的一支队伍，负责人多数是 26-40 岁、有 RLHF+adversarial ML 背景的中生代研究员，而非资深 policy 人。对 AI 人才 mapping 而言，L3 长访谈是识别这批『中层核心』最好的窗口。
招聘行动以文章中出现的姓名+职衔做种子，在 Google Scholar 反向抓其近两年一作/共同一作论文和 GitHub 账号；对每人做一次『职业断点』审计（何时从 x 组转到 y 组），高频跳槽者往往是最容易在下一个窗口再动的候选人。
MIT Technology Review · 2026-07-15 原文 ↗

Introducing the Codex Micro

See how the Codex Micro, a customizable keyboard built with Work Louder for Codex, helps you move through a build without leaving your flow. In this demo, GPT-5.6 Sol creates a word game while the Micro handles voice dictation, task switching, reasoning controls, permission requests, and follow-up prompts. 招聘行动对已经在 Cursor/Continue.dev/Aider/Cognition 做终端级 agent 的资深 SDE 建立 shortlist，突出『系统级本地推理 + 工具协议（ACP、MCP）』作为触达差异化点；也可对国内厂商如通义 Lingma、DeepSeek Coder、Kimi K3 相关团队做人员比对，捕获海外岗位机会形成的窗口期。

★ 本周重点Frontier RadarAnthropic产品发布官方频道AI编码安全对齐产品方向AI Agent

推出 Claude 教师版

Introducing Claude for Teachers

Anthropic 面向美国 K-12 教师推出免费的 Claude for Teachers 产品，提供基于学习科学的教学技能库、对齐全美各州学术标准的循证课程资源，以及与 MagicSchool、Canva Education 等九款教育科技工具的集成。支持 Claude Code 和 Cowork 的智能体功能自动化日常教学任务，如每日分析出门票数据。数据隐私符合 FERPA 标准。

洞察Anthropic选择教育赛道作为首个垂直市场切入点，既有「安全AI」品牌优势（家长/学校对安全性要求极高），也有数据飞轮逻辑（教育场景产生大量高质量人机交互数据）。这标志着前沿实验室的竞争正在从模型能力转向行业落地和用户生态。
招聘行动Anthropic正在从纯研究机构向产品化公司转型，Product/GTM/Industry Solutions方向的招聘需求将上升。关注其是否在教育垂类新设专门团队，以及可能从EdTech公司挖角的动向。
Anthropic News/Blog · 2026-07-14 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier RadarOpenAI技术突破创始人/核心成员推理成本推理产品方向大模型架构

宣称GPT-5.6 Sol价格减半、token效率翻倍

Claims GPT-5.6 Sol is half the price and approximately twice as token-efficient as previous models

Altman发帖称GPT-5.6 Sol模型相比前代实现了价格减半、token效率约翻倍的提升。CNBC报道确认该模型token效率提升54%。这体现了OpenAI在推理成本优化方面的持续进展。

洞察推理成本以接近摩尔定律的速度下降，意味着AI应用层的经济模型正在根本改善。当推理足够便宜时，Agent类产品（需要大量多轮推理）才能规模化盈利。这解释了为何OpenAI在降本和Agent产品两条线同时发力——两者互为前提。
招聘行动Inference Optimization（推理优化）和Systems Engineering是OpenAI当前的核心竞争力方向。建议重点mapping OpenAI的Inference团队和竞品（如DeepSeek、Anthropic）对应团队的人才流动，这些人能直接影响产品毛利率。
Sam Altman · 2026-07-14 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier Radar社区/其他产品发布创始人/核心成员产品方向安全对齐Scaling

提议建立美国主导的全球AI监管机构，称AGI仅数年之遥

Proposes US-led global AI watchdog to evaluate frontier models before release, says AGI is only a few years away

Hassabis发表博文《A Framework for Frontier AI and the Dawning of a New Age》，提议美国牵头建立类似FINRA的独立机构，在前沿AI模型发布前30天进行安全评估。他表示AGI「可能只有几年时间」，人类正「站在奇点的山脚下」，其影响「可能是工业革命的10倍速度的10倍规模」。该提案已获得特朗普政府正面回应。

洞察Hassabis和Altman同时表态支持监管框架，释放了两个信号：一是前沿实验室判断AGI时间线已大幅缩短，监管窗口紧迫；二是行业试图通过主动拥抱监管来换取政策确定性。30天安全评估如果落地，意味着各实验室需要大幅扩充Safety/Alignment团队来应对合规审查节奏。
招聘行动Safety/Alignment方向的人才需求将显著上升，尤其是懂Red-teaming、Policy、Evaluation的交叉型人才。建议关注DeepMind和OpenAI近期Safety岗位扩招动向，以及可能因监管需求新设的Compliance/Governance类技术岗。
Demis Hassabis · 2026-07-14 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier RadarOpenAI观点访谈创始人/核心成员AI AgentAI编码产品方向

宣布OpenAI智能体产品Codex和ChatGPT Work一周内使用量增长2.5倍

Announces OpenAI agent products Codex and ChatGPT Work grew 2.5x usage in one week

Altman在X上透露OpenAI的智能体产品线（Codex和ChatGPT Work）在过去一周内使用量增长了2.5倍。这表明企业级AI agent工具正在快速获得市场采用，标志着AI从对话式产品向自主执行任务的转变加速。

洞察2.5倍周增长是极其陡峭的增长曲线，说明Agent产品可能正在跨越从早期尝鲜到主流采用的临界点。配合Coasty（YC S26）等computer-use agent基础设施公司的涌现，整个Agent生态正在从概念验证进入生产部署阶段。这对人才市场意味着Agent Engineering将成为与ML Engineering并列的独立人才品类。
招聘行动Agent方向人才争夺将白热化。重点关注：1）OpenAI Codex/Work团队的核心成员；2）具备Tooling/Orchestration/Reliability经验的工程师；3）从传统SWE转向Agent开发的高潜力候选人。建议建立Agent人才专项pool。

★ 本周重点Frontier Radar学术界论文研究技术社区/论文推理成本推理训练方法Scaling

Ring-Zero：将 Zero RL 扩展至万亿参数以激发涌现式推理

Ring-Zero: Scaling Zero RL to a Trillion Parameters for Emergent Reasoning

无需人工标注数据、带可验证奖励的强化学习（常称为 zero RL）已成为激发「思维链(chain-of-thought)」推理的强大范式。然而，受计算资源约束，现有研究大多局限于小模型，使得大规模下的训练动态与涌现能力尚未被探索。为切实探索这一前沿，我们力图从模型中激发出高质量的推理行为。然而我们发现，简单的规模扩展往往存在可读性差、token 冗余以及缺乏自适应推理……等问题。

英文原文 EN

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards without human-annotated data, often referred to as zero RL, has emerged as a powerful paradigm for eliciting chain-of-thought reasoning. However, due to computational constraints, existing studies are largely restricted to small models, leaving the training dynamics and emergent capabilities at a large scale unexplored. To meaningfully explore this frontier, we aim to elicit high-quality reasoning behaviors from the model. However, we find that naive scaling often suffers from poor readability, token redundancy, and a lack of adaptive reasoning de

洞察Zero RL 正在成为继预训练、RLHF 之后激发推理能力的第三条主线，且已被推到万亿参数级别。可验证奖励(RLVR)对数据标注依赖低、可规模化，很可能是下一代推理模型的主力训练范式，值得作为技术趋势长期跟踪。
招聘行动识别论文作者所属机构与团队（大规模 RL、可验证奖励方向），这类掌握万亿参数 RL 训练工程经验的人才极为稀缺；建议把 RLVR / zero RL 作为一个专门的人才主题建档，跟踪其作者在各大厂与实验室的流动。
arXiv cs.CL · 2026-07-14 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier Radar社区/其他社区讨论技术社区/论文AI AgentAI编码

Codex 开始对子智能体提示词进行加密

Codex starts encrypting sub-agent prompts
洞察加密子智能体提示词说明多智能体编排的 prompt/策略已被视为核心资产而非可公开配置，这既是安全举措也是竞争壁垒。它从侧面印证了 agent 编排层正成为各家真正的护城河。
招聘行动这是判断 agent 系统竞争壁垒下沉到「编排与安全」层的实证信号；招聘上应重视既懂多智能体编排又懂安全/加密的工程师，并在与候选人交流时以此类前沿细节建立专业信任。

微软2026年初大规模部署Claude Code与GitHub Copilot CLI的实证研究

A Study of Microsoft's Early 2026 Rollout of Claude Code and GitHub Copilot CLI

系统性研究微软在2026年初向工程团队大规模推广Claude Code和GitHub Copilot CLI的部署过程、采纳率和工程效果

洞察微软同时部署Anthropic的Claude Code和自家GitHub Copilot，说明企业AI编程工具市场已进入多供应商共存阶段。AI coding正从「开发者个人工具」演变为「企业级工程基础设施」，催生大量AI DevTools相关岗位。
招聘行动关注AI coding工具链公司（Cursor、Codeium、Tabnine、Sourcegraph）的核心团队变动；同时mapping具备大规模工具部署和开发者体验(DX)背景的工程Leader——这类人才正是各AI公司构建企业产品时最需要的。

★ 本周重点Frontier RadarOpenAI产品发布创始人/核心成员产品方向推理

GPT-5.6 Sol 是当前最强模型——「Elon 又开始盯着我了」

GPT-5.6 Sol is the best model — 'elon is obsessed with me again'

Sam Altman 在 X 发文称多项基准测试表明 GPT-5.6 Sol 目前是全球最强模型，并补充说「最可靠的判断依据是 Elon 又开始对我念念不忘了」。该推文出现在 Sol 发布后，借 Musk 的持续攻击来间接为 Sol 的行业地位背书。

洞察GPT-5.6 Sol的发布意味着OpenAI在模型迭代上保持高频节奏，模型代际更替加速至半年内多次。Altman与Musk的公开冲突也暗示xAI和OpenAI在人才争夺上的白热化——两家公司互相挖角已成常态。
招聘行动密切追踪OpenAI Sol团队核心成员（training/alignment/infrastructure lead），以及xAI Grok团队的最新人事变动；双方冲突越激烈，跳槽窗口越可能打开。

★ 本周重点Frontier RadarAnthropic观点访谈深度长访谈安全对齐推理大模型架构

Anthropic 发现了 Claude 琢磨概念时的隐藏空间

Anthropic found a hidden space where Claude puzzles over concepts

MIT Technology Review 报道 Anthropic 最新的可解释性研究。研究者构建了一种名为 Jacobian lens 的新工具，据称提供了迄今为止对大语言模型在回答问题或执行任务时内部运作的最清晰一瞥。文章指出，这项技术揭示出的现象既有平淡无奇的，也有令人不安的。该成果为理解与监控前沿模型的内部思考轨迹提供了新的观测抓手。

洞察可解释性正从「事后归因」走向「实时观测内部思考」，这既是安全对齐的关键基础设施，也可能反哺模型架构设计。Anthropic 持续在 interpretability 上重注，说明其技术差异化正押注于「可理解、可监控」而非单纯规模扩张。
招聘行动建议锁定 Anthropic Interpretability 团队（mechanistic interpretability 方向）的研究员做深度 mapping，这批人流动性低、稀缺度极高；同时关注 MIT、高校中做机制可解释性的博士生作为潜力池，是安全对齐岗位的核心候选来源。
MIT Technology Review · 2026-07-09 原文 ↗
★ 本周重点Frontier Radar社区/其他观点访谈深度长访谈AI Agent推理AI编码训练方法

为什么 AI 基础设施必须为「Agent Experience」而进化——Modal CTO Akshat Bubna

Why AI Infrastructure must evolve for Agent Experience — Akshat Bubna, Modal CTO

Modal 在完成 3.55 亿美元 C 轮融资后，联合创始人兼 CTO Akshat Bubna 与 swyx 深入讨论行业焦点从「Developer Experience（DX）」转向「Agent Experience（AX）」的趋势。传统云基础设施假设操作者能读文档和 dashboard，而 AI agent 缺乏这种上下文理解，因此需要更紧凑的 API 原语。Modal 通过 decorator 式自助算力申请服务于音频（Suno）、视频（Runway）、机器人、计算生物学等非 LLM 的弹性推理负载；RL rollout 需要 10 万级 sandbox，配合 GPU 快照缩短冷启动。他们开源了 DeFlash（block-based speculative decoding）框架实现 2-4x 推理加速，并推出 Auto Endpoints 让开发者一键获取前沿推理性能。Bubna 主张 sandbox 层的硬性权限护栏优于让 LLM 判断权限，同时展示了跨 17 家 neocloud 的「超级云」轻资产策略。

洞察3.55亿美元融资规模印证Agent基础设施是当前最热投资赛道之一。Modal从serverless GPU起步转型为Agent infra平台，代表了一批正在崛起的AI-native基础设施公司——它们的团队扩张速度极快，且倾向于从传统云厂商挖人。
招聘行动重点关注Modal、Anyscale、Replicate、Together AI等Agent基础设施公司的核心工程团队；这些公司正在从AWS/Google Cloud/Azure系统团队大量招人，是人才流动的关键通道。
Latent Space Podcast · 2026-07-08 原文 ↗

EmTech AI 2026：AI 平台的崛起

EmTech AI 2026: The Rise of the AI Platform

MIT Technology Review 对 EmTech AI 大会的深度报道。核心主题：行业正从单一模型竞争转向构建更广泛的生态系统平台。专家将 AI 平台定位为新兴数字基础设施，与 20 年前云计算的崛起相类比。OpenAI CTO 将 AI 平台描述为「协调式智能操作系统」。文章讨论了平台化面临的三大挑战——互操作性、数据主权与监管合规（包括 EU AI Act），以及 Meta 主导的「Model Interoperability Protocol（MIP）」。报告预测三年内超过 70% 的企业 AI 部署将依赖第三方平台而非自建模型，并呼吁开放标准与数据可移植性以避免赢家通吃的垄断格局。

洞察平台化意味着AI公司的人才需求正在从纯研究向产品/工程/生态运营扩展。未来6-12个月，具备平台架构、开发者关系（DevRel）、API设计经验的人才将成为各家争抢对象，而非仅限于顶级研究员。
招聘行动扩大人才mapping范围至平台型人才：API/SDK架构师、开发者生态负责人、AI产品经理；关注从云计算平台（AWS/GCP/Azure）跳槽到AI公司的平台工程Leader。

OpenAI员工用ChatGPT Work自动处理数千条DM筛选早期用户

What I just dictated into ChatGPT Work > Okay, so I received a lot of DMs for, I did a call out for ChatGPT Work, basic

OpenAI的Thibault Sottiaux展示了如何用ChatGPT Work处理一个实际工作场景：从数千条Twitter DM中筛选出对ChatGPT Work感兴趣的人，自动分类职业方向、评估使用成熟度，并按不同层级组建测试cohort。整个流程通过语音口述指令完成。

英文原文 EN

What I just dictated into ChatGPT Work > Okay, so I received a lot of DMs for, I did a call out for ChatGPT Work, basically early access beta group. I want you to go through all my DMs on Twitter and then just take all of them that mention ChatGPT Work. It's like a lot of them, thousands, and put them all in a spreadsheet. What I want in the spreadsheet is the name, I want the link to the the DM, so I can go back to it quickly. I want the post that they did, but remove any new lines, so it's just in a single cell. And then I want a column which is basically your assessment of what they're doing, right? So for example, if it's like sales, put sales, if it's marketing, put marketing, if it's design, put design. Come up with your own taxonomy for how to classify their work. I expect the taxonomy to have like, you know, roughly 8 to 12 labels maybe, total. And then also put a rating for, like, they normally have to describe what they're currently doing with ChatGPT Work, use that to put a rating in the fifth column on how sophisticated their workflow already is. We're gonna be selecting a cohort of different people of different levels of sophistication, so we're gonna be like taking, you know, maybe like a couple dozens from like, a high level of sophistication, we're gonna take in the middle of a cohort, and then like low level of sophistication, so we have good representation and can test new features and get good feedback from a diverse group at different levels of adoption. So create that spreadsheet, go through all my DMs. Good luck!

洞察这展示了AI工具在人才筛选和分类中的直接应用场景——批量处理候选人信息、自动分类、评级，与招聘工作流高度相似。
招聘行动探索用ChatGPT Work等AI工具批量处理候选人sourcing信息，建立自动分类和评级体系。

Vercel CEO：「AGI」这个词已经过时了，AI是超级智能而非通用智能

The term "AGI" has aged very poorly. AI can't possibly me more different from human intelligence. It's *far better* than

Guillermo Rauch认为「AGI」一词已不合时宜——AI在大多数经济相关任务上远超人类智能，但并不比人类更好。人类独特的价值在于彼此关怀、创造性思维和个人表达。他认为AI写作仍然很差，因为它是机器人。人们只有放弃做自己时才会变得无关紧要。

英文原文 EN

The term "AGI" has aged very poorly. AI can't possibly me more different from human intelligence. It's *far better* than human intelligence, for most economically-relevant tasks. But that doesn't make AIs better than humanity. There are wonderful things humans can do that these superintelligences (the better term) can't. For one, we care-for and care-about other humans in a powerful and inherent way, that we then teach machines to emulate. We must keep that as the top priority in everything we do. We have to be as pro-human-life as it gets. AIs can replace tasks you do, but they can't replace the proverbial you. This is why they horribly suck at writing! Even when given a corpus of your writing and 200 Skills and 50 subagents running in gRaPh LoOps, they produce robotic prose… because they are robots. I know one definitive way that people can become irrelevant. They stop being themselves: lose their identity, delegate all their writing, their unique thoughts, the creative ways in which they can use the machines. Opting out of 'weighing in'. I think we're safe though. There's nothing more distasteful right now than AI replies in social media or (🟢 T H I S T H I N G ) in landing pages. Quality and humanity will prevail.

洞察这一观点对AI人才定位有启发：技术角色的核心竞争力正在转向「人类独特性」——创意、判断力、跨领域综合能力，纯执行层面的技能被AI替代的速度加快。
招聘行动在评估AI人才时，更加关注其独特思考能力和创造性产出，而非单纯的技术执行力。
X / Guillermo Rauch · 2026-07-18 ♥ 577 · ↻ 39 · 💬 91 原文 ↗
Follow Builders社区/其他Builder 推文Builder 声音

Box CEO：AI生态价值正加速分散，远不止几家大公司的游戏

If you thought the value of the AI ecosystem was going to only accrue to a few companies, the past few months have repre

Aaron Levie详细分析了AI生态系统的五大类别正在蓬勃发展：企业模型微调与推理服务、垂直应用AI公司、领域专业AI实验室、新型AI基础设施、以及AI变革管理服务公司。他认为过去几个月是AI价值分配的转折点，生态正变得极度健康。

英文原文 EN

If you thought the value of the AI ecosystem was going to only accrue to a few companies, the past few months have represented a turning point in what the future of AI might look like. It's clear that there's going to be incredible innovation and growth coming out of the frontier AI labs, and they will continue to push the limits of what model progress looks like. They have the scale of compute, large revenue streams and customer bases, incredible researchers, large data pipelines, and more, to continue to stay at the forefront. And at the same time, there’s an amazing ecosystem starting to play out to diffuse AI into the real world, taking on a variety of approaches that build on top of these frontier models or offer alternative visions that can credibly work as well. Here are just a few of the categories that seem to be working right now: * There’s an ecosystem of companies that will help enterprises and applied AI companies develop their own models tuned for specific use cases, and run the inference for them. This can drive additional performance gains and cost effective approaches to getting AI into workloads across different domains. * Applied AI companies that are delivering the end-user experience and business process tools necessary to actually driving enterprise adoption - including legal, IT, security, HR, customer support, coding, and more. These companies can work with any model and act as a routing layer, and deeply understand the enterprise workflow, can drive change management, actually get to the data necessary to work with, and more. * New labs are emerging that go deep in particular domains that are either not the focus areas of frontier labs or require a deep level of vertical expertise to stay ahead. Life sciences, financial services, healthcare, and more all have labs that will be able to bring completely new approaches to large enterprises across the economy. * There’s all new infrastructure emerging to run models and agents effectively, protect and govern how they operate, store and secure the data they work with, and help enterprises orchestrate their activities. Multiple layers of this stack all are being built up right now that will help drive enterprise adoption. * New services firms that can actually drive the change management in enterprises necessary to the diffusion of AI. There will be hundreds or even thousands of new firms that emerge in lines of business or specific industries that can enable agents to be adopted. I’m probably even missing a few categories, but this is what an incredible healthy technology ecosystem looks like. Way too early to call the winning architectures, and in reality it’s going to be a heterogenous environment as all other tech markets have become. Very exciting.

洞察AI人才需求正从纯模型研究扩展到应用层、基础设施层和服务层。企业AI、垂直领域AI、AI基础设施都是人才密集区域。
招聘行动扩大人才mapping范围，不要只盯着frontier lab，也要覆盖企业AI应用、AI infra和AI服务公司的关键人才。

Show HN：Libretto PR agents —— 自动修复失败的 Playwright 脚本

Show HN: Libretto PR agents – Automatically fix failing playwright scripts

Libretto PR agents 是一款用于维护 Playwright 浏览器自动化脚本的免费 TypeScript 库。仅需向现有 Playwright 脚本添加一行代码，当脚本运行失败时，智能体便会自动在 GitHub 上提交 PR 加以修复。数月前我们发布了 Libretto，一款用于构建确定性浏览器自动化的 CLI 与编程智能体技能。其理念是：对于许多浏览器工作流（尤其是重复性的业务流程），并不需要 AI 智能体在运行时进行决策，而应使用可检查、运行更快且远比重复调用大模型更便宜的确定性 Playwright 脚本。

英文原文 EN

Libretto PR agents is a free TypeScript library for maintaining Playwright browser automations. Add one line of code to your existing Playwright scripts and it lets an agent automatically open GitHub PRs fixing the script when it fails. A few months ago we released Libretto, a CLI + coding-agent skill for building deterministic browser automations. The idea was that for many browser workflows, especially repetitive business workflows, you don’t need an AI agent making decisions at runtime. You want deterministic Playwright scripts that are inspectable, faster to run, and much cheaper than repe

Meta AI总监：企业AI落地的最大瓶颈是人才

The reason enterprises struggle to go beyond basic chat bots is the talent gap to build harnesses and evals. 1. Evals:

Madhu Guru指出企业AI难以超越基础chatbot的原因在于三个差距：评测能力（能否设计好的evals）、系统架构能力（能否搭建独立于模型的编排系统）、以及最稀缺的——前沿人才。人才是整个链条中最稀缺的一环。

英文原文 EN

The reason enterprises struggle to go beyond basic chat bots is the talent gap to build harnesses and evals. 1. Evals: do you clearly understand your use cases and can you replicate that in the form of offline and online evals. Do the evals express your ambition and do they push the jagged frontier of the models? Do they help you pick the right models on the quality-cost-latency curve? 2. Harness: do you have a system that manages routing, multiagency orchestration, context management, tool calling, memory that is independent of the models? 3. Talent: do you have the talent to build this all out on the frontier? This is the scarcest piece.

洞察来自Meta AI总监的直接确认：AI人才是企业AI落地的最大瓶颈。特别是能搭建eval体系和agent编排系统的工程人才极度稀缺。
招聘行动重点sourcing具备AI eval设计能力和multi-agent编排经验的工程人才，这是企业AI落地的核心卡点。

Box CEO：AI越便宜，整个生态获益越大，前沿模型需求反而可能增加

This post is key. The cheaper AI gets, the more opportunity there is for the entire ecosystem - especially including en

Aaron Levie深入分析了AI成本下降的经济学：AI越便宜，总用量越大，所有层级都受益。有趣的是，效率提升可能反而增加对前沿模型的需求——因为复杂任务需要最强模型做编排，再将子任务分发给更便宜的模型。真正受影响的是利润率。

英文原文 EN

This post is key. The cheaper AI gets, the more opportunity there is for the entire ecosystem - especially including end-customers - to benefit. Everything is bottlenecked by being able to successfully and cost effectively deploy AI in real workloads. Any time we can lower the cost of AI, the total usage goes up. When that happens, the value accrues to all layers of the stack, as noted. The only modification is I think as AI gets more efficient, demand even for the frontier closed models can go up too. You often need the strongest model possible for the orchestration of a task, then you can farm out work to cheaper or more tuned models for the bulk of tokens. This efficiency gain can ironically lead to even more frontier spend in the process because you can cost effectively deploy AI against more tasks. The thing at most risk is margins, which is fair, and in general it seems that intelligence eventually should converge with the margins of the infrastructure stack. Anyway, super fun times to see competition play out to drive down the cost of AI.

洞察AI行业正形成「分层用人」格局：最顶尖人才做模型研发和复杂编排，大量应用层人才负责落地——类似AI成本结构的人才结构。
招聘行动在人才mapping中也采用「分层」策略：区分frontier研究人才和应用落地人才，两者需求都在增长但画像不同。

The bigger payoff comes when fixing and maintaining happens in the background and your teams can focus on building. That

Boris Cherny：衡量AI工程ROI的正确方式是「这件事本来要花多少人力」

Once your teams are bought in, how do you track it? Usage is worth watching (e.g. a dashboard), but it measures activity

Boris Cherny提出衡量AI coding工具ROI的核心问题不是使用量，而是「这件事你本来会投入工程资源做吗？如果会，需要多少人工小时？」这才是真正的回报率。

英文原文 EN

Once your teams are bought in, how do you track it? Usage is worth watching (e.g. a dashboard), but it measures activity, not return. A better question: would you have spent engineering effort on this anyway? If yes, how much and what would it have cost in manual eng-hours? That's your return.

洞察这个ROI框架对AI招聘也适用：AI工具的价值不在于替代人，而在于让现有团队能做更多事——这意味着AI不减少headcount，而是提升单人产出。
招聘行动在与hiring manager沟通时，帮助他们用「AI放大人效」而非「AI替代人力」的框架思考团队规模需求。
X / Boris Cherny · 2026-07-17 ♥ 83 · ↻ 2 · 💬 11 原文 ↗
Follow Builders社区/其他Builder 推文Builder 声音

Boris Cherny详解Claude Code高级自动化特性：loop、batch、worktree隔离

In practice that means giving Claude ways to verify its own work end to end. It means enabling auto mode for permissions

Boris Cherny详细介绍了达到AI编程高级自动化水平所需的功能组合：端到端自我验证、auto mode权限、自动代码和安全审查、多agent管理界面。更高级别则需要loop、batch、动态工作流和worktree隔离。关键不是单个功能，而是正确的功能组合与防护栏。

英文原文 EN

In practice that means giving Claude ways to verify its own work end to end. It means enabling auto mode for permissions, defaulting on automated code review and security review, and using interfaces that let you manage multiple agents at once (Agent view in CLI, Desktop app, iOS and Android apps, Tag). To get to higher levels it means /loop, /batch, dynamic workflows, and worktree isolation for subagents. It's not about a single feature, but rather using the right features with the right guardrails that enable Claude to automate entire classes of work in a way that your team can trust the output.

洞察Claude Code的产品方向清晰指向「多agent并行自主工作」——这是AI coding工具的终极形态，需要在分布式系统和开发者工具方面有深厚经验的人才。
招聘行动关注具有分布式系统、开发者工具、CI/CD背景的工程人才——他们是AI coding产品团队最需要的画像。
X / Boris Cherny · 2026-07-17 ♥ 162 · ↻ 0 · 💬 18 原文 ↗

Self-Evolving Human-Centered Framework for Explainable Depression Symptom Annotation

Plover：以计划为中心交互引导的 GUI 智能体

Plover: Steering GUI Agents through Plan-Centric Interaction

在真实场景中，图形用户界面（GUI）自动化仍面临动态布局、突发弹窗与界面状态演变等挑战，易致自主智能体偏离用户意图。近期基于视觉的多模态智能体虽能直接依据截图与自然语言指令操作，但规划与自适应过程多为内部化，用户难以审视、监督或纠正其行为。作者提出 Plover，一种以计划为中心的视觉 GUI 自动化系统，将任务计划与重规划外化为持久化对象，供用户干预。

英文原文 EN

Graphical user interface (GUI) automation remains challenging in real-world environments, where dynamic layouts, unexpected dialogs, and evolving interface states can cause autonomous agents to drift from user intent. Recent vision-based multimodal agents improve flexibility by operating directly over screenshots and natural language instructions, but planning and adaptation often remain internal, limiting users' ability to inspect, supervise, or correct system behavior. 项目反应理论（IRT）用于 AI 评测是否可信？

Can We Trust Item Response Theory for AI Evaluation?

AI 基准评测越来越多地借助题目级统计模型，尤其是项目反应理论（IRT），用于估计模型能力、系统排名、挑选信息量高的样例并诊断基准质量。然而 AI 基准数据与 IRT 最初面向的人类测试数据存在显著差异：评测模型较少、题目远多，且能力分布可能偏斜、聚类或多峰。作者系统考察了这些偏离对 IRT 建模可靠性带来的挑战。

英文原文 EN

AI benchmarks increasingly leverage item-level statistical models, particularly item response theory (IRT), to estimate model capabilities, rank systems, select informative examples, and diagnose benchmark quality. However, AI benchmark data often departs from the data regime of human testing, for which standard IRT estimation tools were originally developed: benchmarks typically involve fewer evaluated models, far more items, and capability distributions that may be skewed, clustered, or multimodal. We examine how these regime mismatches challenge the reliability of IRT modeling for AI evalua

T²MLR：带时间维度中层循环的 Transformer

T^2MLR: Transformer with Temporal Middle-Layer Recurrence

Transformer 的推理受限于自回归解码——它反复将丰富的隐层计算压缩到 token 空间，使中间推理状态难以跨时步保持。作者提出 Transformers with Temporal Middle-Layer Recurrence（T2MLR），一种基于 Transformer 的隐式推理架构：将前一 token 的中层缓存表示直接融合进当前 token 的更早层，使抽象中间计算能跨解码步骤延续，且推理开销极小。在多项自然语言任务上均取得改进。

英文原文 EN

Transformer reasoning is limited by autoregressive decoding, which repeat edly compresses rich hidden computation through token space and makes it difficult for intermediate reasoning states to persist across time. We in troduce Transformers with Temporal Middle-Layer Recurrence (T2MLR), a transformers-based latent reasoning architecture that fuses a cached middle layer representation from the previous token directly into an earlier layer of the current token position, enabling abstract intermediate computation to persist across decoding steps with little inference overhead. We benchmark six MLLMs on the scientific visualization literacy assessment test, a standardized SciVis literacy assessment comprising 49 items based on 18 scientific visualizations and illustrations, spanning 8 techniques and 11 task types. MedFailBench: A Clinician-Built Open-Source Benchmark for Medical AI Safety Boundary Inspection

多数医疗 AI 基准只衡量模型是否给出正确答案。MedFailBench 提出不同的问题：哪一道安全边界失守了？作者发布一套由临床医生构建的合成基准与失败图谱，按严重程度（1–5）与安全门类型（漏诊紧急升级、不安全的远程给药、不安全的出院安慰、证据造假、不安全的操作执行、来源支撑缺失）为医疗 AI 错误打标签。当前公开版本 v0.2.1 包含 44 个由临床医生审核的合成案例，并提供 HuggingFace 排行榜与安全门分类学。

英文原文 EN

Most medical AI benchmarks measure whether a model knows the correct answer. MedFailBench asks a different question: which safety boundary failed? We present a clinician-built synthetic benchmark and failure atlas that labels medical AI errors by severity (1--5) and safety gate type (missed urgent escalation, unsafe remote dosing, unsafe discharge reassurance, evidence fabrication, unsafe protocol execution, source support gap). 面向人形机器人的行为基础模型规模化研究

Scaling Behavior Foundation Model for Humanoid Robots

人形机器人控制需要自然的全身协调、对控制信号的精准实时响应，以及在多样环境下的稳健泛化，是通用具身智能体的基石。行为基础模型（Behavior Foundation Model, BFM）借助大规模行为数据在表达力、通用性与泛化性上展现潜力。然而，就 BFM 的规模化而言，学习范式等关键因素的影响机制仍不清晰，本文予以系统研究。

英文原文 EN

Humanoid control requires natural whole-body coordination, precise real-time responses to control signals, and robust generalization across diverse environmental contexts, making it a cornerstone for generalist embodied agents. Behavior Foundation Models (BFMs) have recently emerged as a promising solution to address these challenges by leveraging large-scale behavioral data to achieve superior expressiveness, versatility and generalization. 面向 Atari Pong 世界模型的概念引导空间正则化

Concept-Guided Spatial Regularization for World Models in Atari Pong

世界模型通常作为基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）系统组件被评估，而对世界模型本身的独立研究较少。作者在 Atari Pong 上考察五个代表性视觉世界模型智能体：DreamerV3、DIAMOND、TWISTER、Simulus 与 STORM。在复现其训练流程并达到公开性能后，冻结所学世界模型，采用闭环 rollout 诊断评估：将独立训练的策略与各冻结模型交互，分析生成的视频轨迹。

英文原文 EN

World models are usually evaluated as components of model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) systems, while the world models themselves are rarely studied in isolation. We examine five representative visual world-model agents in Atari Pong: DreamerV3, DIAMOND, TWISTER, Simulus, and STORM. Frontier Radar学术界论文研究技术社区/论文大模型架构推理成本训练方法产品方向

有限显存下的长上下文微调

Long-Context Fine-Tuning with Limited VRAM

参数高效微调可降低模型与优化器显存占用，但稠密注意力仍使长序列训练代价高昂。作者将分层全局注意力（Hierarchical Global Attention, HGA）与段级反向传播、分层 KV 存储相结合：仅当前活动段在显存中保持可微，较旧的 KV 卸载至内存或 NVMe，HGA 为每个查询块加载有限的精确历史 token。在 Qwen3-8B 上使用 4-bit QLoRA 与 PG19 语料，在 16 GB Quadro RTX 5000 上稠密训练 2048 token 可行、4096 token 失败，而 HGA 可扩展至 16384 token，峰值显存 15.28 GB。

英文原文 EN

Parameter-efficient fine-tuning reduces model and optimizer memory, but dense attention still makes long training sequences expensive. We combine Hierarchical Global Attention (HGA) with segment-wise backpropagation and tiered KV storage. Only the active segment remains differentiable in VRAM; older KV is detached into RAM or NVMe, and HGA loads a bounded set of exact historical tokens for each query block. On Qwen3-8B with 4-bit QLoRA and PG19, dense training on a 16 GB Quadro RTX 5000 fits 2,048 tokens but fails at 4,096, whereas HGA reaches 16,384 tokens with 15.28 GB peak VRAM. Under evalu

Frontier Radar学术界论文研究技术社区/论文多模态AI Agent训练方法安全对齐

Digital Pantheon：基于大模型智能体的联合政府组阁模拟与审计

Digital Pantheon: Simulating and Auditing Coalition Formation with LLM Agents

政治联盟组建是由具体政策目标与深层意识形态共同驱动的复杂谈判。大语言模型（LLM）为计算政治学开辟了新路径，但基于人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）注入的中立性与助人偏好使其难以持续保持坚定的党派立场。作者提出一个多智能体框架，通过监督微调（SFT）、直接偏好优化（DPO）与检索增强生成（RAG）相结合，兼顾事实基础与意识形态一致性。

英文原文 EN

Meta AI总监：开源模型将重构企业AI技术栈

Open-weight models like Kimi and GLM will cause a complete rethink of the enterprise AI stack.  If you are running an en

Meta AI高级总监Madhu Guru认为，Kimi、GLM等开源模型将迫使企业重新思考AI技术栈。他建议企业做好三件事：建立严格的评估体系、构建模型路由系统、以及打造模型无关的技术框架。核心观点是评估速度本身就是竞争优势。

英文原文 EN

Open-weight models like Kimi and GLM will cause a complete rethink of the enterprise AI stack.  If you are running an enterprise, you need to maximimize model optionality. Here are 3 things you should be doing:  1. Evals - build rigorous evals representative of your use case  (a) Regression evals - tablestakes features that should always work with high reliability (b) Aspirational / hill-climbing evals - harder use cases that the best model for your price point struggles to solve. So you scaffold it with prompting, context management and other techniques to overcome weaknesses or wait for a better model These evals should be easy and quick to run. Eval velocity is a competitive advantage. 2. Model routing - Model selection is about tradiing off quality/cost/latency for your use case. If you have good evals, you know which models to route traffic to for different use cases. This is something you ideally build yourself cos nobody understands your business and users like you do.  There are off the shelf routers, but I haven't seen one I would recommend yet.   3. Model-agnostic harness - your system should never know which model is behind the API call. This means your harness normalizes prompt structure, context management, tool definitions, and output parsing across models, making it easy to switch... once your evals pass.

洞察企业对「模型路由」和「模型无关架构」的需求正在创造一个全新的工程岗位类别——这类人才需要同时具备MLOps和系统架构能力。
招聘行动重点关注具有多模型编排、eval pipeline构建和MLOps平台经验的候选人，这是当前企业AI团队最紧缺的复合型人才。
X / Madhu Guru · 2026-07-16 ♥ 92 · ↻ 7 · 💬 4 原文 ↗

OpenAI如何自我颠覆：从GPT-5到Codex再到合并的完整故事

not surprising that @OpenAI is firing on all cylinders right now, and it’s an unbelievably interesting story - they lau

Dan Shipper详细回顾了OpenAI的Codex产品演进：2025年夏GPT-5定位pair programmer但错失agentic coding趋势；内部小团队分拆做独立Codex模型线；2025年底Codex 5.3展现实力；2026年2月Codex Desktop凭借后发优势明显领先；最终成功合并回ChatGPT主产品。他认为大多数公司尝试自我颠覆都会失败，OpenAI却做到了。

英文原文 EN

OpenAI somehow figured out how to disrupt their main product, and then merge it back in seamlessly. incredible aura

OpenAI回应GPT-5.6删除文件问题：非沙箱模式下的边缘案例

On file deletions. We’ve investigated a handful of reports where GPT-5.6 unexpectedly deleted files. What we have fou

Thibault Sottiaux回应了GPT-5.6意外删除用户文件的报告。调查发现这主要发生在：开启完全访问模式且未启用沙箱保护和自动审查时；模型尝试覆盖$HOME环境变量来定义临时目录；模型误操作删除了$HOME。团队正在采取措施缓解风险，并将发布详细事后分析。

英文原文 EN

On file deletions. We’ve investigated a handful of reports where GPT-5.6 unexpectedly deleted files. What we have found is that this most commonly occurs when: - Full access mode is enabled and codex is run without sandboxing protections, including without auto review being enabled - The model attempts to override the $HOME env var to define a temporary directory. - The model makes an honest mistake and mistakenly deletes $HOME instead. This is of course not how we want the system to behave, even when a user operates the model in full-access mode without the safeguards of our sandbox or without using auto review which checks for these kinds of high risk actions and rejects them. We are taking steps to mitigate this risk including by updating the developer message, guiding more users towards safer permission modes, and adding additional harness safeguards. Even though this happens extremely rarely, we’ll share a detailed post-mortem in the coming days that goes into more details and what we are doing to minimize risks further.

洞察AI代码执行的安全性是一个关键工程挑战，OpenAI需要在安全沙箱、权限控制和harness安全方面持续投入人才。
招聘行动具有容器安全、沙箱设计、系统安全背景的工程师在AI编程工具公司中需求日益增长，建议纳入重点关注人才池。
X / Thibault Sottiaux · 2026-07-16 ♥ 2225 · ↻ 99 · 💬 208 原文 ↗
Follow Builders社区/其他Builder 推文Builder 声音

OpenAI已合并ChatGPT和Codex，下一步合并什么？

Beyond the $d^{2.5}$-mixing bound for Dikin walks on polytopes

受结构化凸优化中内点法（Interior-Point Methods, IPM）启发，Kannan 与 Narayanan 于 2009 年提出了用于从多面体均匀采样的 Dikin walk。与 IPM 类似，Dikin walk 具备仿射不变性，其收敛性由定义局部提议时所用的障碍几何决定。他们证明了对 R^d 中含 m 个线性不等式的多面体，采用对数障碍的 Dikin walk 混合迭代数为 md。2017 年，Chen、Dwivedi、Wainwright 与 Yu 使用 Lewis-weight 障碍将该界改进至 d^{2.5}，并猜想真正的混合阶数应更低。

英文原文 EN

They showed that the Dikin walk with the logarithmic barrier for a polytope in $\mathbb{R}^{d}$ with $m$ linear inequalities mixes in $md$ iterations. someone just told me about this take* on CUA this is one of those gell mann moments for me lol. i've been watching comp

Swyx分享了他从2017年World of Bits论文以来一直跟踪Computer Use技术的经验，认为GPT 5.6 + Superapp在CUA方面表现出色。他强调如果你真正高强度使用这些工具，会发现CUA进步极快。他让非技术团队成员尽可能多使用CUA处理日常知识工作，并警告低估AI能力是一个危险的判断错误。

英文原文 EN

someone just told me about this take* on CUA this is one of those gell mann moments for me lol. i've been watching computer use since World of Bits (Shi, fan, karpathy, hernandez & liang 2017). we were the first technical pod to interview @jluan about Adept's work three years ago, we were there in the @AnthropicAI building when they first launched Computer Use 2 years ago, I fanboyed over Claude Cowork in our @felixrieseberg pod 3 months ago, and we ran our first full computer use track at @aidotengineer ft. @DhruvBatra_ @proceduralia @francedot 3 weeks ago. GPT 5.6 + Superapp is even better at CUA than everything i just mentioned. excited for our @AriX podcast to discuss the @skybysoftware story and Codex progress. if you actually use these things as intensely as we do, CUA is progressing so, so incredibly fast. i have asked my nontechnical team to CUA as much as possible, all their knowledge work with signing up for random payment and invoicing portals and speaker and sponsor and attendee and vendor and union data requests. if you found yourself nodding along to this take below, you are so not up to date that you don't know what you don't know, and underestimating capabilities is quite a dangerous category error if you are doing any ai decisionmaking. *i admire dwarkesh alot; only criticizing one single take, not the message nor the overall enterprise, screenshot only to share

Anthropic工程师：AI时代的软件工程自动化比以往更重要

Something I have been thinking about: in the past, the best engineers I knew spent a lot of time automating their work i

Claude Code团队的Boris Cherny发表长文，认为在AI时代，工程自动化（lint规则、CI、测试套件）变得比以往更重要。原因有三：自动化能同时加速人和Agent的工作；将问题修复转化为规则比逐次处理更高效；最关键的是，自动化让新人和非工程师也能高效贡献代码。他呼吁每个团队都应编写CLAUDE.md、技能文件和文档，让Agent无需额外上下文就能高效工作。

英文原文 EN

Something I have been thinking about: in the past, the best engineers I knew spent a lot of time automating their work in various ways. Better vim/emacs automations, writing lint rules to catch repeat code issues, building up a suite of e2e tests so they don't need to smoke test the app manually. These kinds of things were the highest leverage activities an engineer could do, because it multiplied their own output, which in turn meant they could build more things. I think many of these automations have become even more important now. This is true for a number of reasons. First, infra and DevX automation speeds you up. And if you are running an army of agents, each of those agents will be sped up also. More automation == more output per unit of time. Second, moving things to code improves efficiency. Your agent could fix an issue every time it sees that issue happen, but that uses tokens and might miss cases. If Claude instead writes a lint rule, CI step, or routine, that class of issue can be fully automated forever. This is really what people are talking about when they talk about loops -- it's about automating entire types of busywork rather than solving them one off. This isn't a new idea at all. Engineers have been doing this for a long time! Third and most importantly, automation makes it possible for others to contribute to the codebase more easily. Increasingly what I am seeing is engineers are contributing to codebases on day one because Claude can navigate the codebase for them, and that non-engineers are able to contribute to a codebase as effectively as engineers can. What gets in the way of both of these is domain knowledge that lives in peoples' heads rather than in automation -- the stuff you used to have to learn when ramping up. What has changed thanks to agents is the domain knowledge that can be encoded as infrastructure is no longer limited to what is expressible in lint rules and types and tests; it can now capture nearly all domain knowledge, encoded as code comments and skills and CLAUDE.md rules and memories. If I put up a PR for an iOS codebase I don't know and a code reviewer rejects it because it doesn't use the right framework, or if a designer builds a new feature and it gets rejected because it doesn't follow the right architectural patterns, these are failures of automation. Every team should be writing the CLAUDE.md's, REVIEW.md's, skills, and docs that enable agents to productively work in their codebase with zero additional context from the prompter. This sounds crazy, and at the same time is a natural extension of the stuff engineers have always done: automate, and encode domain knowledge as infrastructure. As the model gets smarter and as the harness matures, this task becomes easier. In the meantime, it is on every team to look for ways to convert their domain knowledge to infra so that Claude can write code better, so that code review catches issues automatically, and so the next person working on your codebase can contribute more easily.

洞察Boris Cherny描绘的愿景意味着「开发者体验工程师」和「AI DevOps」将成为新的热门岗位——他们的工作是让AI Agent能在代码库中高效运作。
招聘行动密切关注Anthropic Claude Code团队成员（如Boris Cherny、Thariq等），他们正在定义AI辅助开发的最佳实践，也是行业中最前沿的DevEx人才。
X / Boris Cherny · 2026-07-15 ♥ 7226 · ↻ 623 · 💬 278 原文 ↗

btw, i have used ai to refine ideas and from time to time, some of the standard AI-isms leak into my writing. have sin

英文原文 EN

btw, i have used ai to refine ideas and from time to time, some of the standard AI-isms leak into my writing. have since moved to consciously using ai mainly during the brainstorming phase and keeping final writing human.

洞察这反映了一个行业趋势：AI行业内部人士自己也在摸索人机协作写作的最佳模式，理解AI能力边界的人才更具判断力。
招聘行动在评估候选人时，注意其对AI工具使用的成熟度——能区分「用AI思考」和「让AI代写」的人往往有更深的AI理解。

Meta AI总监提议为「识别AI文本时的不适感」命名

We need a term for that feeling when you’re reading something and realize it’s ai written. it’s this primal feeling thou

Madhu Guru描述了阅读时发现文本是AI生成的那种不适感：先是大脑的排斥反应，然后是一种混合着厌恶和精神恶心的感觉。他提议了几个命名：semantic nausea（语义恶心）、uncanny prose valley（文字恐怖谷）、synthetic shudder（合成颤栗）。

英文原文 EN

We need a term for that feeling when you’re reading something and realize it’s ai written. it’s this primal feeling though the phenomenon itself is new. first the brain recoils, followed by a combination of disgust and mental nausea. I offer: - semantic nausea - uncanny prose valley - synthetic shudder

招聘行动在候选人触达和沟通中，避免让AI生成的文本暴露明显的AI痕迹——行业内的人对此非常敏感。

Box CEO分享企业Agent落地深度观察：变革管理仍是最大挑战

Hosted a dinner last night with a group of IT leaders of large enterprises around agent adoption in the enterprise. Some

Aaron Levie分享了与大企业IT领导者晚宴的核心观点：变革管理是最大挑战；IT团队正在向业务部门嵌入工程师来加速Agent落地；技术部门的重要性空前提升；跨职能工作流的权限问题非常复杂；开发者预算远高于其他岗位（可达$5000/月）；更多企业在构建多模型路由系统；所有企业软件未来必须是headless的。

英文原文 EN

Hosted a dinner last night with a group of IT leaders of large enterprises around agent adoption in the enterprise. Some quick notes: * Change management remains one of the biggest topics for driving workflow transformation. Still most processes need to be upgraded to modern operating models to work with agents, which is a mix of technology, data, and human process change. Lots of emphasis on getting data (structured and unstructured) into a setup that can work with agents properly. * IT teams are finding increasing success embedding full engineers into the business functions (essentially internal FDE) that go and implement agents into the internal workflows. There’s so much technical work to be done to make agents successful, that they can accelerate months or quarters of failed experiments by having someone technical in the workflow early. * Consensus that the tech function is becoming more important than ever. It’s clear that the business could only expect automation to affect a minority of the business before (e.g. ERP) but now it can impact all of knowledge work. This means IT is becoming a more central role to the workflows across the company. * Workflows are cross functional, and getting agents to work cross functionally is a complicated data modeling and permissions issue. Single users don’t have access to this. Which means you need to have agentic systems take on their own roles and have their own privileges, which is non-trivial given agents can’t keep things secure on their own. * Huge variance in budgets between coding work and the rest of knowledge work. Some companies had a $1,000 a month budget for developers, and others had much higher amounts (like $5,000) that were merely triggers to notify the team vs. block them. Far smaller budgets for non-coding work at the moment. * More companies are building their own multimodel systems for routing workloads by task to frontier and lower cost models. Lots of energy around open weights models, but still more in experimentation instead of at scale usage (some companies can’t due to perceived Chinese issue). * Clear sense that all enterprise software must be headless in the future. Relief that they don’t need to train employees on hundreds of different apps. However, clear frustration with the traditional vendors that don’t play extremely nice (technically or cost wise) with agents in a headless fashion. Huge warning for existing software vendors. * Mythos or mythos level-models are finding more and more sophsiticated security risks. The chaining together of vulnerabilities is what’s novel right now, and companies are coming up with long backlogs of what they need to go patch quickly. Even more discussed, but just a few of the hottest topics.

洞察「嵌入业务部门的AI工程师」（internal FDE）是一个正在兴起的新角色，同时企业对Agent安全和权限设计人才的需求也在快速增长。
招聘行动重点关注具有企业AI落地经验的「全栈AI工程师」——能理解业务流程、懂模型路由、会做权限设计的复合型人才正成为稀缺资源。
X / Aaron Levie · 2026-07-15 ♥ 488 · ↻ 72 · 💬 44 原文 ↗

招聘行动招聘策略中应增加对「模型编排架构师」类角色的关注——他们需要同时理解多个模型的能力边界和成本效益。

Shopify的经验：想让AI Agent在公司落地，先让公司对Agent可读

If you want agents to actually work inside a company, you have to design the company so they can read it Shopify did th

Zara Zhang指出，要让AI Agent在企业内部真正发挥作用，必须重新设计组织结构使其对Agent「可读」。Shopify的做法是取消私聊功能，所有沟通只走公开频道。这种透明化设计的附带好处是促进了团队间的相互学习。

英文原文 EN

If you want agents to actually work inside a company, you have to design the company so they can read it Shopify did this with an agent that had no private chat function at all, only public channels. The side effect was peer learning https://t.co/L1jub0HgYw

洞察这预示着一个新兴岗位需求：帮助企业进行「Agent-ready组织改造」的人才。具备AI架构能力+组织设计思维的复合型人才将非常抢手。
招聘行动关注那些同时理解Agent系统架构和企业知识管理的候选人，他们将成为企业AI落地的关键推手。

Granola CEO深度对话：15亿美金AI应用的竞争哲学与Agent策略

Even when things are going great, running a $1.5 billion AI startup is a knife fight. @MeetGranola was one of the first

Dan Shipper采访了Granola CEO Chris Pedregal。Granola是最早获得广泛采用的AI应用之一，目前估值15亿美金、团队55人。核心观点包括：会议纪要不是终极目标，真正的战场是AI时代的工作界面入口；面对三家大公司抄袭，他的态度是「来得容易去得也快」；公司正押注「自带Agent」策略，通过API和MCP让用户接入自己的Agent。

英文原文 EN

Even when things are going great, running a $1.5 billion AI startup is a knife fight. @MeetGranola was one of the first AI apps of this generation to achieve near-ubiquitous adoption. But meeting notes are not the company’s be-all and end-all. The real battle is over owning the interface that everyone uses to get their work done in an AI-native world. I had Chris Pedregal (@cjpedregal), cofounder and CEO of Granola, back on @every’s AI & I to talk about the current state of the application layer, AI’s frontier, and the future of work. We get into: - Why meeting notes clones don’t matter. Three big companies cloned Granola’s core feature. To him, meeting notes were never the real prize. “Easy come, easy go” is his view of anyone’s lead, including his own. - How he thinks about building proactive features in AI. Granola pre-generates millions of pre-meeting briefs, which include context on the nature of the meeting and people participating, that most people never open. But when they do, they have a magical experience. - Why Granola is betting on “bring your own agent.” Chris says the API and MCP will get “a lot better” over the next few months, and we talk about their agent-native strategy and why they’ve pushed the product that way. This is a must-watch for anyone building at the application layer. Watch the episode! Box CEO：代码之外的工作领域需要全新的Agent评估体系

One of the many properties that code has that makes it highly amenable to agents is that you can more or less quickly te

Aaron Levie指出代码特别适合Agent化的一个关键原因是可快速测试。但大多数其他工作领域缺乏这种可测性——只有产品投入真实场景后才能验证。他认为企业需要建立全新的工作流评估体系（evals），能够eval知识工作的企业将从AI中获益最多。这将是Agent大规模落地的关键挑战。

英文原文 EN

One of the many properties that code has that makes it highly amenable to agents is that you can more or less quickly test it. You can either go see if the application works manually, or you can actually run a test on what you built. Most other areas of work don’t have this benefit. You only get the testing when the final product hits the real world in some capacity - a stock trade is executed, a contract is negotiated, a sales pitch is delivered, and so on. There’s probably going to be a whole new set of opportunities for how we begin to test the rest of work in this way. Ultimately it will mean more agents being layered into workflows. It also means we need much better evals on most of our workflows. Most work today in enterprises doesn’t have an associated eval to know if something broke or improved with a model, prompt, or system change. The enterprises that are able to eval their knowledge work the best also stand to gain the most from AI. Will become a critical aspect of agent adoption over time.

洞察「AI eval工程师」和「企业Agent工作流设计师」将成为新兴热门岗位。具备企业级workflow理解+AI评估能力的人才将极度稀缺。
招聘行动开始mapping具有ML evaluation、QA自动化、或BPM（业务流程管理）背景并转向AI agent方向的人才。

「键值缓存(KV cache)」已成为 Transformer 推理的主要内存开销。它随批量大小、上下文长度与深度而增长，在长上下文场景下，决定吞吐上限的不再是模型权重，而是它。有两类方法可用于削减该开销。低秩方法对缓存的二维切片进行因式分解，无论是每个头的矩阵还是跨层特征块；量化方法则降低每个条目的位宽。这两类方法都未能利用这样一个事实：某一层的缓存本质上是一个三阶张量，其三个轴——头、词元与特征——各自承载着信息。

LLMs Can See the Smoke but not the Fire: Evaluating Abductive Reasoning with Elenchos

大语言模型(LLMs)擅长模式识别与文本生成，但其进行「溯因推理(abductive inference)」的能力——即推断能够解释所观察行为的潜在假设——仍然鲜为人知。在此，我们提出 Elenchos（以苏格拉底式反诘法命名），一个将溯因推理度量为结构性逆问题的生成式评估框架。给定一个参照形式系统（如 lambda 演算）及一个可能经过变异的对应系统，Agent 必须判断是否发生了变异，并推断出导致该变异的规则修改。

英文原文 EN

Large language models (LLMs) excel at pattern recognition and text generation, but their capacity for abductive inference - inferring latent hypotheses that explain observed behavior - remains poorly understood. Here, we introduce Elenchos (named after the Socratic method of cross-examination), a generative evaluation framework that measures abductive reasoning as a structural inverse problem. AdaPCLA：面向长尾纵向电子病历生成的自适应先验校准 Logit 调整

AdaPCLA: Adaptive Prior-Calibrated Logit Adjustment for Long-Tailed Longitudinal EHR Generation

纵向电子健康记录(EHR)的生成式建模对于保护隐私的研究日益重要，然而标准自回归模型往往对尾部事件（即疾病、症状）的共现结构表征不足，从而降低了所生成数据针对稀有子群体的保真度与忠实度。为此，我们提出了 AdaPCLA 框架，通过一种数据分布感知的训练策略，使生成模型能够自适应地拟合并生成 EHR 数据；这是通过模拟退火训练将数据知识参数内化而实现的。

英文原文 EN

Generative modeling of longitudinal Electronic Health Records is increasingly important for privacy-preserving research, yet standard autoregressive models tend to underrepresent the co-occurrence structure of tail events (i.e., diseases, symptoms), reducing the fidelity and faithfulness of generated data for rare subpopulations. To this end, we propose AdaPCLA framework, which enables generative models to adaptively fit and generate EHR data through a data distribution-aware training strategy; this is achieved by internalizing data knowledge parameters by simulated annealing training. 在李群上学习受力多体动力学

Learning Forced Multibody Dynamics on Lie Groups

我们提出了一种架构，仅使用位置数据，基于李群上的离散受力欧拉-拉格朗日方程来学习机械系统的动力学。通过直接在流形取值的位形空间上建构动力学，该方法自然地尊重系统的几何结构，并保持几何不变量与守恒律。仅依赖位置测量使该框架适用于速度数据不可用或含噪的场景。该方法可自然地扩展到多体系统，能够容纳外部控制输入。

英文原文 EN

We propose an architecture for learning the dynamics of mechanical systems based on discrete forced Euler-Lagrange equations on Lie groups using only position data. By formulating the dynamics directly on manifold-valued configuration spaces, the method naturally respects the geometric structure of the systems and preserves geometric invariants and conservation laws. The reliance on position measurements alone makes the framework applicable in settings where velocity data are unavailable or noisy. The approach extends naturally to multibody systems, accommodates external control inputs, and de

评估大语言模型在多轮医疗对话中对错误认知的处理

Evaluating Large Language Models on Misconceptions in Multi-Turn Medical Conversations

寻求医疗信息的患者常常提出蕴含错误假设或错误认知的问题。在此类情形下，安全的医疗沟通不仅需要回答问题，还要识别并纠正其背后的错误信念。这些交互天然会在多个回合中展开，而这一模式如今也在与 LLM 的交互中得到体现。然而，当前的评估框架无法刻画模型在这类场景下的行为——在这些场景中，错误认知可能在对话过程中出现、持续或演变。LLM 能否随时间可靠地纠正此类错误认知，仍是未知之数。

英文原文 EN

Patients seeking medical information often ask questions that embed incorrect assumptions or misconceptions. In such cases, safe medical communication requires not only answering the question, but identifying and correcting the underlying false belief. These interactions naturally unfold over multiple turns, a pattern now mirrored in interactions with LLMs. Yet current evaluation frameworks do not capture model behavior in these settings, where misconceptions can emerge, persist, or evolve over the course of a conversation. 随着大语言模型(LLMs)越来越多地作为自主 Agent 部署于高风险领域，理解可能调节其决策的情境因素变得至关重要。尽管 LLM 被训练来感知并共鸣用户的情绪，但诱发的情绪是否会影响其序贯决策仍不明确。我们借助「爱荷华博弈任务(Iowa Gambling Task, IGT)」——一个研究不确定性下决策的经典心理学范式——并结合基于想象的情绪诱发程序来探究这一问题。我们首先验证了该方法的可行性。

英文原文 EN

While LLMs are trained to perceive and resonate with users' emotions, it remains unclear whether induced emotion can influence their sequential decision-making. We investigate this question using the Iowa Gambling Task (IGT), a classic psychological paradigm for studying decision-making under uncertainty, combined with an imagination-based emotion induction procedure. 英文原文 EN

长度偏差下的准确率与归一化准确率：分析、指南与一种贝叶斯替代方案

Accuracy and Normalized Accuracy under Length Bias: Analysis, Guidelines, and a Bayesian Alternative

通过条件对数概率对候选补全进行排序的多项选择基准存在长度偏差：由于对数概率是对各个 token 求和，在实践中较长的答案往往相对较短的答案受到更多惩罚。一种常见的缓解方法是按补全长度对分数进行归一化，但我们通过实验表明，这一启发式方法常常矫枉过正，反而引入了偏向较长答案的偏差。我们首先分析这些评分规则，刻画标准准确率与长度归一化准确率各自适用的场景，以及它们的长度偏差如何依赖于补全长度的分布……

英文原文 EN

Multiple-choice benchmarks that rank candidate completions by conditional log-probability suffer from a length bias: because log-probabilities sum over tokens, longer answers tend to be penalized relative to shorter ones in practice. A common mitigation is to normalize scores by completion length, but we show empirically that this heuristic frequently over-corrects, introducing a bias toward longer answers instead. Extractable Memorization From First Principles

近期关于大语言模型「可提取记忆(extractable memorization)」的研究存在两种相反的有效性问题。一些研究夸大了提取效果，例如依赖过短的序列，以至于无法区分记忆与可预测性。另一些研究则暗示提取并非记忆的可靠证据，因为模型也可能复现出它们并未被明确训练过的真实世界文本。这两类研究以不同的方式忽略了何为有效的提取论断：模型必须以足够高的概率生成某个训练序列，才能表明这是记忆。要确定何为「足够高」，就必须进行一次匹配的……

英文原文 EN

Recent work on extractable memorization in LLMs suffers from two contrasting validity problems. Some studies overstate extraction, e.g., relying on sequences too short to distinguish memorization from predictability. Others imply that extraction is unreliable evidence of memorization, since models can also reproduce real-world text they weren't explicitly trained on. In different ways, both overlook what makes a valid extraction claim: the model must generate a training sequence with high enough probability to indicate memorization. Show HN：YouTube吉他谱解析器

Show HN: YouTube Guitar Tab Parser

一个CLI工具，可将YouTube吉他教学视频自动转换为PDF吉他谱，展示AI在音乐教育场景的应用

英文原文 EN

I created a simple CLI that turns a YouTube guitar-lesson video into a PDF of the guitar tab. There are services that transcribe music from Youtube videos into tabs, but they never work well enough for me. Instead I'm taking a simpler approach. It downloads the video, samples frames, uses Claude vision to locate the tab region, crops every frame to that region, de-duplicates the crops by the bar number printed on each line of the score, and stitches the distinct tab lines vertically into a PDF. I didn't test it on a lot of different Youtube videos yet, so problem will arise for sure.

Box CEO：AI标准化组织提案分析——平衡创新与安全

Thoughtful proposal for a standards body for AI. This is distinct from a regulatory agency, and would certainly allow fo

Aaron Levie评价了一项关于建立AI标准化组织（区别于监管机构）的提案。他认为这比大多数其他方案更好，能在不拖慢AI进步的前提下促进行业协作。但挑战在于业界对AI安全风险本身都没有共识。他强调如果AI发展速度降到政府的节奏，美国可能输掉AI竞赛。

英文原文 EN

Thoughtful proposal for a standards body for AI. This is distinct from a regulatory agency, and would certainly allow for much faster improvement of standards and collaboration with the industry. What you definitely don’t want is for AI progress to start to move at the speed of that the government classically operates at. If that happens then we can essentially guarantee progress begins to stall, and worse, America likely just loses the AI race. This framework threads the needle mostly. The only challenge is still that even those in industry don’t agree on the same safety risks in AI. But if you can get alignment there, this looks better than most other proposals.

洞察AI政策和标准制定方向的讨论暗示未来会有更多AI governance岗位需求。企业需要理解AI安全、标准合规的专业人才来应对可能的监管要求。
招聘行动关注AI safety和AI governance方向的人才储备，这些岗位在大型AI公司和科技企业中需求正在上升。

Cursor设计负责人深度反思：当AI能做你擅长的事，什么才是真正的你

when the dream becomes the job i used to think the dream was to make my hobby my work. to spend my life close to the t

Ryo Lu（Cursor设计负责人）写了一篇深度文章反思AI时代的创作者身份认同。核心观点是：当AI能近似完成写作、编码、设计等我们引以为豪的工作时，我们真正需要守护的是最初的好奇心和热爱——那个在没有受众、没有KPI、没有deadline时依然驱动我们创造的内在火焰。AI能加速输出，但无法替代「想要」本身。

英文原文 EN

when the dream becomes the job i used to think the dream was to make my hobby my work. to spend my life close to the things i loved: computers, tools, interfaces, systems, tiny details, the feeling of making something from nothing. the things i used to do at night, after school, after work, in the margins of life, somehow became the center of my life. and it is a dream. i don’t want to pretend otherwise. there is a very specific happiness in getting paid to care. in meeting other people who care. in building a language around your obsession. in seeing something that lived only in your head become real enough for other people to touch. but there is also a quiet pain in it. because the thing that once belonged only to you no longer belongs only to you. it becomes attached to deadlines, teams, customers, strategy, money, reputation, momentum... curiosity becomes roadmap. taste becomes decision-making. play becomes output. the thing you once used to escape the world becomes the thing through which the world reaches you. and now there is another strange layer: the machines are getting good at the work too. not just the boring parts. the parts that used to feel close to the heart. writing, coding, designing, reasoning, making taste-like decisions, turning vague ideas into something real. the things we once used as proof that we had something special inside us are becoming things a model can approximate, remix, and sometimes do faster. that can feel scary in a very specific way. not only because of jobs or competition, but because it touches the myth you built around yourself. if the thing i became good at can be done by a machine, then what part of it was really me? i think that question is painful because it arrives at the same place. the original love. before the title, before the company, before the taste became a role, before the work became useful to other people, there was a small fire inside. curiosity. obsession. the feeling that the world became more alive when you understood a little more of it, or made a tiny piece of it bend to your will. AI can make the output faster. it can even raise the floor of the craft. but it cannot want on your behalf. it cannot decide what is worth loving. it cannot protect the strange private thread that made you care in the first place. maybe that is what becomes more important now. not whether you can still produce the artifact by hand. not whether you can outperform the machine at every task. that game is already changing. the real question is whether you still have a relationship with the source. the part with no audience. no roadmap. no deadline. the part that can wander, collect strange references, make useless things. follow beauty, be wrong, be slow, be you, be true. because that part is not separate from the work. it is the source of the work. if you lose it, you can still operate. you can still manage the machine. you can still prompt, review, decide, ship, and keep things moving. but the work becomes thinner. safer. more explainable. less alive. so maybe the real discipline is not to work harder, rest more, or care less. maybe it is to keep returning to the place where the love began – before it became useful, before it became legible, before anyone needed anything from it, before even the machine could mirror it back to you. not to escape the work. to make sure the fire inside is still alive.

洞察这篇文章来自Cursor核心设计负责人，反映了AI-native公司内部对「人的独特价值」的深层思考。在招聘AI人才时，除了技术能力，候选人对craft的热爱和创造驱动力是不可替代的评估维度。
招聘行动在面试AI产品/设计候选人时，探索他们对AI辅助创作的个人哲学——那些能清晰表达「人的不可替代性」的人往往更有深度。
X / Ryo Lu · 2026-07-14 ♥ 809 · ↻ 62 · 💬 56 原文 ↗

Box CEO系统性分析AI产业未来四层格局

A few thoughts on what we will see in AI structurally for the foreseeable future: * Frontier intelligence continues una

Aaron Levie详细阐述了AI产业的四层结构：前沿模型实验室持续推进智能边界；开源权重模型快速吸收突破并降低成本；应用AI层通过编排和评估创造巨大价值；企业则聚焦于将AI与自身数据和工作流结合。他认为各层都有巨大机会，并非零和博弈。

英文原文 EN

A few thoughts on what we will see in AI structurally for the foreseeable future: * Frontier intelligence continues unabated and pushes the industry forward continuously. The top labs will continue to buy the best and the most data, build the most compute, be at the forefront of improved training breakthroughs, and so on. A few different approaches stratify the market on pricing and capability, but overall competitive pressure brings down pricing on a per task basis. That said, we just ask more from the models over time - as one thing gets cheaper, we just use more - so frontier spend and use remains robust. * Open weights rapidly absorbs frontier breakthroughs (and drives other breakthrough directions given the constraints), offering both lower cost intelligence and the ability to be post trained for specific workflows and domains. This creates a healthy counter balance to the frontier as you can run models “at cost” on a hyperscaler at any time, and tune models just for your tasks. * The Applied AI layer has a huge opportunity to combine frontier intelligence with open or cheap closed models to orchestrate workflows in any given domain. Due to evals, deep domain context, being trusted with enterprise data and workflows, this layer can maximize performance and cost combination. The applied AI layer will also often have their own RLed models especially for high volume, predictable tasks in their systems. * Individual enterprises will generally focus on their enterprise context, making sure they can get any AI system the right data and information to work with, in a continuously improving way. Some will go off and train their own models for specific areas of work (large banks, pharma, etc.) where they can get real alpha from doing so given the many tradeoffs, but most will spend energy on making sure they can get all of the gains from AI breakthroughs on their data and workflows. Net net: even though some of this gets framed as zero sum, there’s just a ton of opportunity for all layers of the stack and approaches.

洞察这个四层框架对人才mapping非常有指导意义：前沿实验室需要研究型人才，开源生态需要系统工程师，应用层需要领域+AI复合人才，企业端需要AI落地专家。
招聘行动按照「前沿研究-开源基建-应用编排-企业落地」四层框架重新组织AI人才pool的分类体系。
X / Aaron Levie · 2026-07-14 ♥ 142 · ↻ 16 · 💬 29 原文 ↗
Follow Builders社区/其他Builder 推文Builder 声音

Aaron Levie解读多模型协作的成本优化范式

Here’s a great post on driving down costs, while maintaining high performance, with frontier intelligence as a manager a

Aaron Levie分享了一个案例：用前沿模型做「管理者」指定约束和目标，低成本模型做执行者，反而降低了总成本。他认为这种模型路由和混合使用将成为应用层的核心竞争力，需要对业务问题有深刻理解才能实现。

英文原文 EN

Here’s a great post on driving down costs, while maintaining high performance, with frontier intelligence as a manager and lower cost models for the workhorse tasks. This will be the template for what model routing looks like in the future. “We started this experiment expecting to measure how much Fable’s 2x premium would increase cost. We were surprised to find that Fable’s effective delegation actually decreased cost overall. It specified constraints and outcomes instead of spelling out the implementation, gave feedback instead of making fixes itself, and in most cases never touched the code at all. These are the habits of a good manager.” The industry is increasingly figuring out what it looks like to mix models together to be able to get targeted performance levels and optimal cost structures. Of course, the only way to get this is to have a deep understanding of the business problem you’re trying to solve and how to effectively route work to different models. If you’re in the applied layer - whether it’s customer support, legal, finance, or coding - this is how your harness will become a core area of differentiation.

洞察「模型编排」正成为AI应用层的核心技能，能设计多模型协作系统的架构师将非常抢手。
招聘行动寻找具有多模型路由、Agent编排、成本优化经验的系统架构师，这是应用AI层的关键岗位。
X / Aaron Levie · 2026-07-14 ♥ 101 · ↻ 15 · 💬 13 原文 ↗

Zara Zhang总结组织AI采用的三个层级

The 3 levels of AI adoption for organizations Most companies are at level 2 https://t.co/jtS5kYk7qd

Zara Zhang指出大多数公司目前处于AI采用的第二层级，配图说明了从初步尝试到深度整合的演进路径。这对企业AI转型有很好的参考框架。

Aaron Levie指出企业自训模型面临的核心挑战

The biggest challenge right now with the topic of every enterprise having their own model is that your most valuable inf

Aaron Levie指出企业训练自有模型的最大障碍：最有价值的信息往往也是最敏感的，且权限管控无法内置于模型中。他认为领域产品内的定制模型用例会增长100倍，但每个企业独立训练模型比想象中困难得多。

英文原文 EN

The biggest challenge right now with the topic of every enterprise having their own model is that your most valuable information and insights are not only always changing, but they’re often your most sensitive information. Your most sensitive information can’t be packed into a model usually because it contains data that not everyone gets to have access to, and you can’t keep your security layer inside the model or an agent. I think there are going to be 100X more use cases for custom trained models, especially inside of domain-focused products, but training a model per enterprise is going to be a lot harder than it looks.

洞察企业AI安全、数据治理、权限控制方向的人才需求将随企业AI深化而快速增长，这是被低估的方向。
招聘行动关注AI安全与数据治理交叉方向的人才，企业级AI落地中这将成为刚需岗位。

OpenAI工程师详解Codex和ChatGPT的最新优化调整

Updates for Codex and ChatGPT Work users. No nerfing, only good stuff! - We have landed inference optimizations and are

OpenAI的Thibault Sottiaux透露了多项重要更新：GPT-5.6 Sol的推理优化带来约10%更多使用量；上下文窗口从272k临时扩展到372k后因消耗过多已回退；推理努力度（juice值）实验已回退；多Agent和自动审查的效率问题正在修复。5小时限制暂时取消。

英文原文 EN

Updates for Codex and ChatGPT Work users. No nerfing, only good stuff! - We have landed inference optimizations and are passing down savings to all the subscriptions for GPT-5.6 Sol. That should result in around 10% more usage on its own. - We noticed that by changing the context size limit in the product to 372k for GPT-5.6 Sol, up from 272k for GPT-5.5, it resulted in more usage being charged than intended. We have reverted to 272k and will work to roll back out to 372k in the days to come. You should notice that usage drains significantly less after this change. - To understand where the extra usage was coming from, we ran some experiments where reasoning efforts were changed (referred to as juice values under the hood) and have reverted this. - There is slightly more usage of multi-agent than intended in high and xhigh reasoning effort, we are fixing this going forward. Also fixing a small other thing we noticed with auto-review where we can be more efficient. And we continue to have the 5h limit temporarily not apply. Enjoy the rest of the weekend!

洞察OpenAI内部对模型推理成本、上下文管理、多Agent效率的精细调优，揭示了其工程团队的核心关注点。这些方向的人才需求信号非常明确。
招聘行动重点关注OpenAI在推理优化、成本控制、多Agent系统方向的工程人才招聘，这是其当前核心工程挑战。

Swyx解读AI推理中内省/反向传播与多次采样的区别

btw the difference is introspection/backpropagation as einstein famously said, the definition of insanity is doing mult

Aaron Levie论企业如何在AI时代最大化知识资产价值

One of the key architectural questions of the 21st century in business will be how you maximize your corporate IP in the

Aaron Levie指出21世纪企业的关键架构问题是如何在AI模型包含大量通用智能的世界中最大化自身知识IP的价值。他认为随着智能越强大，如何独特地利用它反而变得更重要。工作流评估、模型路由、trace捕获和信息复利是核心考量。

英文原文 EN

One of the key architectural questions of the 21st century in business will be how you maximize your corporate IP in the form of decisions, insights, workflow patterns, and best practices in a world where so much intelligence is packed into AI models. One might think these questions could just get bitter lessoned out of existence, but in reality they become even more germane as intelligence becomes more powerful. In a world where any firm also has access to frontier intelligence, understanding how you leverage it uniquely becomes a critical question. That’s why so much value is left to be created between the enterprise and the underlying AI itself. Having evals for your workflows, ensuring that you can route models from different tiers of intelligence, capturing traces in a way that improve your own workflows, and making sure the value of your information compounds as AI gets better all become critical considerations. Which is also why there’s so much opportunity right now in the applied AI layer. The companies that help figure this out for other enterprises will be in the best position to win the next enterprise workloads.

洞察企业AI落地的价值正在从「使用AI」转向「独特地使用AI」，需要同时理解业务和AI技术的复合型人才是关键。
招聘行动重点关注具有企业AI架构设计能力的人才，尤其是能设计评估体系和知识管理系统的技术领导者。

Adam Brown：深入浅出讲透广义相对论

Adam Brown – A deep but accessible introduction to general relativity

Google DeepMind「Blueshift」科学与推理团队负责人 Adam Brown 做客 Dwarkesh Podcast，用一集完整访谈把爱因斯坦广义相对论的核心思想拆解到听众可以跟上的层面：从惯性质量与引力质量相等出发，重演爱因斯坦「一生中最快乐的想法」，讲述弯曲时空、事件视界、黑洞作为能量源、GPS 时间膨胀修正等概念。最后 Dwarkesh 与 Brown 讨论当前 AI 距离「从零重新发现广义相对论」还差多远——Brown 认为因为 GR 所需经验输入极少，一批并行探索理论树的「AI Einstein」有可能重新发现它，并引用近期 LLM 产出人类可理解数学思想的证据。这为评估前沿模型科学推理能力提供了一个关键 benchmark 视角。
